# [Universal - Transfers and Payments: SWIFT & WISE Available Currencies and limits](https://app.getguru.com/card/cexBaa5i/Universal-Transfers-and-Payments-SWIFT-WISE-Available-Currencies-and-limits)

<section class="ghq-card-content__callout" data-ghq-card-content-type="CALLOUT" data-ghq-color="purple" id="TLRdjB5WJRZG" style="background-color: #9013fe24;">
 <p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph align-center" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" data-text-align="center" id="7xd90xffJDTP">
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   <span class="ghq-card-content__text-color" data-ghq-card-content-type="TEXT_COLOR" style="color:#2f3ba2">
    üåéThis is a universal article and includes information that is applicable for both Wio Business and Wio Personal products.
   </span>
  </strong>
 </p>
</section>
<h1 class="ghq-card-content__large-heading" data-ghq-card-content-type="LARGE_HEADING" id="pqNfA3IBc5bZ">
 Topic Overview
</h1>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="CvngZX2sHL7I">
 This article is a guide for understanding Wio's international payment offerings, the usage and limitations of different currencies, and the operational processes governing these transactions. Customers should be encouraged to stay informed about policy changes and to utilize available resources for any queries or issues that may arise.
</p>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph ghq-is-empty" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="P5ZdhbPlR056">
</p>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="pRuD7TJRDF5c">
 <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
  Currency Processing Methodologies:
 </strong>
</p>
<ul class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST">
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="3zNjBRjwlPkz">
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   SWIFT Transactions
  </strong>
  : Major currencies such as Euro (EUR), British Pound (GBP), and US Dollar (USD) will be processed via the SWIFT network. This ensures standardized and secure international money transfers for these key currencies.
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="qXmDixtLyZbn">
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   Wise Transactions
  </strong>
  : Other countries local currencies, including the Canadian Dollar (CAD) and Argentine Peso (ARS), will be processed through Wise. It is important to note that Wio Multi Currency accounts will exclusively handle SWIFT transfers, while Wise payments are limited to accounts using AED (United Arab Emirates Dirham).
 </li>
</ul>
<hr class="ghq-card-content__horizontal-rule" data-ghq-card-content-type="DIVIDER"/>
<h1 class="ghq-card-content__large-heading" data-ghq-card-content-type="LARGE_HEADING" id="rPPvJuhrfJCj">
 Saudi Riyal (SAR) &amp; Indian Rupee (INR) through SWIFT
</h1>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph ghq-is-empty" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="7o2Fx1e79Aev">
</p>
<h2 class="ghq-card-content__medium-heading" data-ghq-card-content-type="MEDIUM_HEADING" id="Qi7XSNx45wdB">
 <span class="ghq-card-content__text-color" data-ghq-card-content-type="TEXT_COLOR" style="color:#9013fe">
  Saudi Riyal (SAR)
 </span>
 <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   rollout through SWIFT
  </strong>
 </strong>
</h2>
<ul class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST">
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="85KN81bMniVi">
  Available through
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   ALL
  </strong>
  accounts
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="TxlQ9dh3xphF">
  Payment Route:
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   SWIFT
  </strong>
  only
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="G2HlXP5FjDnA">
  Correspondent bank name:
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   First Abu Dhabi Bank - Saudi Arabia
  </strong>
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="vZpN6zXTnnyz">
  Customer can choose
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   SAR
  </strong>
  as transaction currency and initiate the transaction.
  <br/>
 </li>
</ul>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="vnc5VHV7sxT5">
 <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
  SAR Payment cut off time:
 </strong>
</p>
<ul class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST">
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="MRfJ4B9cIDVY">
  Turn Around Time (TAT) is 3 to 5 working days
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="3ZwLFRoO3xG3">
  Non-STP takes longer time, based on clarity required for compliance team - Internal only
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="DVQdv7LJ719i">
  In case customer is getting any problem related to
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   SAR
  </strong>
  please ask customer to Update the APP and it should solve the issue
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="bNjWoZFHlkDK">
  If updating the application is not solving the problem please raise a technical ticket as per
  <a class="ghq-card-content__guru-card" data-ghq-card-content-type="GURU_CARD" data-ghq-guru-card-id="9febb4fc-ae8b-4175-af7b-c95caedd550e" href="https://github.com/RabboPasch/guru-to-github/blob/main/collections/WIO%20PERSONAL/%F0%9F%91%A8%F0%9F%8F%BC%E2%80%8D%F0%9F%92%BBUniversal%20-%20Handling%20Tech%20Issues%20Reported%20by%20Customers/universal-handling-tech-issues-reported-by-customers.md" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
   üë®üèº‚ÄçüíªUniversal - Handling Tech Issues Reported by Customer
  </a>
  <br/>
 </li>
</ul>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="bvc3zh8K1Bia">

  Wio transfer fees for SAR

 <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
  INR Payment cut off time:
 </strong>
</p>
<ul class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST">
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="VXVTwPhsnx0c">
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   Weekdays
  </strong>
  : if the transaction is initiated after 3:30 pm UAE time, amount should be credited, next day before 11 AM UAE time.
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="DWPpX21PeWv5">
  On
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   Saturdays
  </strong>
  if the transaction is initiated please advise customer to expect the transaction by Monday before 11 AM UAE time (As Sunday is holiday for Kotak swift).
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="12vF9NkD3mnO">

   INR
  </strong>

 </li>

<h2 class="ghq-card-content__medium-heading" data-ghq-card-content-type="MEDIUM_HEADING" id="POhv8tRnfC3j">
 Wise Transfers: Available Currencies Sheet &amp; Requests Handling
</h2>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph ghq-is-empty" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="Nl1kfMWLhvUD">
</p>
<h3 class="ghq-card-content__small-heading" data-ghq-card-content-type="SMALL_HEADING" id="kNyrF1btlJhv">
 üìäWise Transfers: List of available countries and currencies sheet
</h3>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="zsh31HLXTIIc">
 <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
  <span class="ghq-card-content__text-color" data-ghq-card-content-type="TEXT_COLOR" style="color:#9013fe">
   This chart includes the list of countries and their respective local currencies to which Wio Business &amp; Wio Personal customers can send funds internationally.
  </span>
 </strong>
</p>
<ul class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST">
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="TpnpRxj1DJp5">
  üí°
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   Multi-Currency accounts (USD, EUR, GBP)
  </strong>
  will only handle international transfers using the
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   <span class="ghq-card-content__text-color" data-ghq-card-content-type="TEXT_COLOR" style="color:#66a030">
    SWIFT
   </span>
  </strong>
  system;
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   <span class="ghq-card-content__text-color" data-ghq-card-content-type="TEXT_COLOR" style="color:#2f3ba2">
    Wise international payments
   </span>
  </strong>
  are only for local transfers in other countries through AED accounts.
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="ApUZrReL1tmn">
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   Wise international payment will handle other countries local currencies transfers.
  </strong>
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="033XdZmyJRov">
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   Example: CAD
  </strong>
  - Canadian Dollar,
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   ARS
  </strong>
  - Argentine Peso , etc. will be processed through
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   Wise Payments
  </strong>
  .
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="72NXLz1obRmp">
  üí°
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   Transactions = Transfers = Payments
  </strong>
 </li>
</ul>

<hr class="ghq-card-content__horizontal-rule" data-ghq-card-content-type="DIVIDER"/>
<h3 class="ghq-card-content__small-heading" data-ghq-card-content-type="SMALL_HEADING" id="yPJ551fjEj3f">
 <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
  üìûWise Payments Related Service Requests (SR)
 </strong>
</h3>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="lQADJbpUTS5X">
 Below are the steps for customer requesting Swift Copy for transfers made through Wise Payments, Or requests regarding delayed Wise Payments, Wise Payments Recall or Amendments requests, here are the steps:
</p>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph ghq-is-empty" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="7DphpZzyJlkJ">
</p>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="Khih4dxZNfaN">
 <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
  <span class="ghq-card-content__text-color" data-ghq-card-content-type="TEXT_COLOR" style="color:#9013fe">
   Wio Care Steps:
  </span>
 </strong>
</p>
<ul class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST">
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="ylFGFur382aF">
  Create a manual case
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="X1ZbVP30vloj">
  Copy and Paste the transfer details from the transactions tab
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="6lMLFC7kbLDP">
  Write the detailed case notes as per your conversation with the customer
 </li>
</ul>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="9er5HzrGotfn">
 <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
  <span class="ghq-card-content__text-color" data-ghq-card-content-type="TEXT_COLOR" style="color:#9013fe">
   For escalated cases
  </span>
 </strong>
</p>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="JZitD5rhXiP9">
 1st: Send email to
 <a class="ghq-card-content__link" data-ghq-card-content-type="LINK" href="mailto:partnersupport@wise.com">
  partnersupport@wise.com
 </a>

 <a class="ghq-card-content__link" data-ghq-card-content-type="LINK" href="mailto:amil.guliyev@transferwise.com">
  amil.guliyev@transferwise.com
 </a>
 &gt; and CC your Team Leader.
</p>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph ghq-is-empty" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="wZnWJJxdXD1N">
</p>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="LqrvuGmnfiZG">

  <span class="ghq-card-content__text-color" data-ghq-card-content-type="TEXT_COLOR" style="color:#9013fe">
   Case assignment and TAT:
  </span>

</p>

<h1 class="ghq-card-content__large-heading" data-ghq-card-content-type="LARGE_HEADING" id="BRleOcru1tPt">
 Outward Available Currencies for SWIFT &amp; WISE Payments
</h1>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph ghq-is-empty" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="5T6mtHdPlZNr">
</p>
<h2 class="ghq-card-content__medium-heading" data-ghq-card-content-type="MEDIUM_HEADING" id="9rCUhbRlR3ZT">
 SWIFT Transfers: List of available countries and currencies sheet Outward Available Currencies Matrix
</h2>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="x3AW915luz9p">
 <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
  Scope
 </strong>
 : Retail, SME
</p>
<ul class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST">
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="BHJGtJNhbAaj">
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   Transactions = Transfers = Payments
  </strong>
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="TVsThXNve1Rv">
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   EEA = European Economic Area
  </strong>
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="TVsThXNve1Rv">
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   Send =
  </strong>
  Outward Transfer
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="d3ckY5R5j2kq">
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   Receive
  </strong>
  = Inward Transfer
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="tLx1JB39Lpjh">
  Applicable for both Wio Business &amp; Wio Personal
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="ztbZfvDPHVFF">
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   Strikethrough
  </strong>
  <del class="ghq-card-content__strikethrough" data-ghq-card-content-type="STRIKETHROUGH" style="text-decoration:line-through">
   strikethrough
  </del>
  countries are temporary un-available
 </li>
</ul>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph ghq-is-empty" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="thCzAwJCfKgY">
</p>
<ul class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST">
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="jBQcnpTN83N7">
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   <span class="ghq-card-content__text-color" data-ghq-card-content-type="TEXT_COLOR" style="color:#66a030">
    Countries marked as "Yes" indicate that
   </span>
  </strong>
  they are available in both the Wio Business and Wio Personal applications for sending and receiving funds.
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="XdLBpBDRTrXR">
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   <span class="ghq-card-content__text-color" data-ghq-card-content-type="TEXT_COLOR" style="color:#ff8a60">
    Countries marked as "No" Indicate that
   </span>
  </strong>
 </li>
 <ul class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST">
  <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="P6yAxIKjXm4G">
   Countries marked as 'NO' will not be displayed in either the Wio Business or Wio Personal applications. customers will be unable to send or receive funds from/to these countries.
  </li>
  <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="03koq2cRSFck">
   This should not be regarded as a technical issue
  </li>
 </ul>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="KrHczrsQsuC2">
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   In case Customer Asks or complain about the unavailability of a restricted country, we can mention to them:
  </strong>
  <em class="ghq-card-content__italic" data-ghq-card-content-type="ITALIC">
   "Currently we will not be able to process the transfer to these countries due to changes in our internal policies".
  </em>
 </li>
</ul>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph ghq-is-empty" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="rILB3MwDPClO">
</p>

<hr class="ghq-card-content__horizontal-rule" data-ghq-card-content-type="DIVIDER"/>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="BSl5uajlPJFh">
 <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
  <span class="ghq-card-content__text-color" data-ghq-card-content-type="TEXT_COLOR" style="color:#ff8a60">
   üõëStrictly for internal consumption: Can a customer who's nationality is Russian or Kazakh initiate payments to Cyprus or Georgia?
  </span>
 </strong>
</p>
<ul class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST">
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="0jdFuNp7svt5">
  If the customer's nationality is 'Russian' or 'Kazakh', they will not be able to initiate transactions to 'Cyprus', 'Georgia', or 'Ukraine'.
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="85QXboZr7xOb">
  There is a high likelihood that these countries may not be available in the selection list, prompting customers to call. In such instances, it is advisable to limit the amount of information provided.
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="PXb81ERZnG3X">
  If a customer calls with related complaints, you will be able to view the customer's nationality in the customer 360 view and manage their expectations accordingly.
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="WDJPJ2RTxynb">
  The rule also applies to SMEs regarding Ultimate Beneficial Owners (UBOs). If the Authorized Individual or any of the UBOs is of the aforementioned nationalities, the rule will be enforced.
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="nWVTjNbiD939">
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   When addressing customers, the response should be:
   <br/>
  </strong>
  <em class="ghq-card-content__italic" data-ghq-card-content-type="ITALIC">
   "Currently we will not be able to process the transfer to these countries due to changes in our internal policies".
  </em>
 </li>
</ul>
<hr class="ghq-card-content__horizontal-rule" data-ghq-card-content-type="DIVIDER"/>
<h2 class="ghq-card-content__medium-heading" data-ghq-card-content-type="MEDIUM_HEADING" id="7kNrJEDtWFHB">
 <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
  üìûSWIFT Payments Related Service Requests (SR)
 </strong>
</h2>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="7kNrJEDtWFHB">
 Below are the steps for customer requesting Swift Copy for transfers made through SWIFT Payments, Or requests regarding delayed SWIFT Payments, SWIFT Payments Recall or Amendments requests, here are the steps:
</p>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph ghq-is-empty" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="V2jbNKyXL3D2">
</p>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="htMF7jNInvTV">
 <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
  <span class="ghq-card-content__text-color" data-ghq-card-content-type="TEXT_COLOR" style="color:#9013fe">
   Wio Care Steps:
  </span>
 </strong>
</p>
<ul class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST">
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="5NGZtDF2dPKk">
  Create a manual case
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="nzCN5TrPjdNT">
  Copy and Paste the transfer details from the transactions tab
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="WpDdDP2vHgRq">
  Write the detailed case notes as per your conversation with the customer
 </li>
</ul>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph ghq-is-empty" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="FHIFRArbPtjZ">
</p>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="7G5zMh5VD9an">
 <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
  <span class="ghq-card-content__text-color" data-ghq-card-content-type="TEXT_COLOR" style="color:#9013fe">
   Case assignment and TAT:
  </span>
 </strong>
</p>

     <td class="ghq-card-content__table-cell" data-ghq-card-content-type="TABLE_CELL">
      <p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph">

     </td>
     <td class="ghq-card-content__table-cell" data-ghq-card-content-type="TABLE_CELL">
      <p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph">

     </td>
     <td class="ghq-card-content__table-cell" data-ghq-card-content-type="TABLE_CELL">

      </p>
     </td>
     <td class="ghq-card-content__table-cell" data-ghq-card-content-type="TABLE_CELL">

       <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
        3 business days
       </strong>
      </p>
     </td>
     <td class="ghq-card-content__table-cell" data-ghq-card-content-type="TABLE_CELL">

<h1 class="ghq-card-content__large-heading" data-ghq-card-content-type="LARGE_HEADING" id="FjDnVeBjyd0C">
 Application Features
</h1>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph ghq-is-empty" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="loLjvXhMG1LZ">
</p>
<h2 class="ghq-card-content__medium-heading" data-ghq-card-content-type="MEDIUM_HEADING" id="bhjtfs0jzPdi">
 Credit Confirmation for Local Transfers
</h2>
<ol class="ghq-card-content__numbered-list" data-ghq-card-content-type="NUMBERED_LIST" start="1">
 <li class="ghq-card-content__numbered-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="NUMBERED_LIST_ITEM" id="rM70rSoha0ZL">
  Once the funds have been credited to Bene, we will send a push notification to the customer indicating that the transaction has been credited.
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__numbered-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="NUMBERED_LIST_ITEM" id="Hf10INLnDtfS">
  Additionally, the transaction history will reflect the status of this transaction as "Credited."
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__numbered-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="NUMBERED_LIST_ITEM" id="rvHt4RJVHZpy">
  Approximately 5 - 6% will not receive a credit confirmation from the Central Bank (CB).
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__numbered-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="NUMBERED_LIST_ITEM" id="VpEsPLgbCz1F">
  If a customer reaches out to check
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   <span class="ghq-card-content__text-color" data-ghq-card-content-type="TEXT_COLOR" style="color:#2f3ba2">
    Beneficiary Claim Non-Receipt
   </span>
  </strong>
  <span class="ghq-card-content__text-color" data-ghq-card-content-type="TEXT_COLOR" style="color:#2f3ba2">
   <span class="ghq-card-content__text-color" data-ghq-card-content-type="TEXT_COLOR" style="color:#2f3ba2">
    (BCNR)
   </span>
  </span>
  , please check the status of the transaction.
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__numbered-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="NUMBERED_LIST_ITEM" id="JXTgH9sxH7V5">
  The
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   "Completed"
  </strong>
  status indicates that Wio has sent the transaction to the Central Bank, but the Beneficiary Bank has yet to send the credit confirmation.
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__numbered-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="NUMBERED_LIST_ITEM" id="7ZxBxL7BJjdP">
  The
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   "Credited"
  </strong>
  status signifies that the beneficiary bank has successfully credited the transaction to the beneficiary account specified by the customer.
 </li>
</ol>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph ghq-is-empty" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="p35ZNaRzJ91F">
</p>
<h2 class="ghq-card-content__medium-heading" data-ghq-card-content-type="MEDIUM_HEADING" id="YXLDmjtPPbV8">
 How to download SWIFT copy through Wio Business &amp; Wio Personal application
</h2>
<ul class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST">
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="1XHK05dTBfVv">
  Available in Transaction history for all Wio customers.
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="3p78ql1ZFrCp">
  customer can get the Swift copy for
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   Old transaction too
  </strong>
  .
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="3rH5bxXVLZfP">
  copy will be available for Local, SWIFT, Wise outward transaction.
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="tHq8MnNBWFhT">
  Customer can get
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   Correspondent bank
  </strong>
  details and
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   UETR number
  </strong>
  in copy itself (applicable only for SWIFT).
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="NTTUuTwpHtDx">
  Same copy will be available in transaction Email we are sending to customer (for all, wise, swift, local).
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="j6OjNUxuNupt">
  Customers must have latest application release to get the option through the app.
 </li>
</ul>
<hr class="ghq-card-content__horizontal-rule" data-ghq-card-content-type="DIVIDER"/>
<section class="ghq-card-content__callout" data-ghq-card-content-type="CALLOUT" data-ghq-color="pink" id="T3hX41nT7eFq" style="background-color: #f9367929;">
 <h1 class="ghq-card-content__large-heading" data-ghq-card-content-type="LARGE_HEADING" id="85KN81bMniVi">
  üõ†Ô∏èPayment Related Checklist &amp; Troubleshooting Guide
 </h1>
 <h2 class="ghq-card-content__medium-heading" data-ghq-card-content-type="MEDIUM_HEADING" id="rfa5WxbUWzx7">
  üìò Introduction
 </h2>
 <p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="12vF9NkD3mnO">
  Customers may report issues related to payments‚Äîsuch as withdrawal restrictions or currency transfer errors. This guide helps FO agents quickly identify the root cause and follow a clear SOP to resolve or escalate the issue efficiently.
 </p>
 <h2 class="ghq-card-content__medium-heading" data-ghq-card-content-type="MEDIUM_HEADING" id="HqnHRHj4r9gX">
  üìå Key Scenarios
 </h2>
 <ol class="ghq-card-content__numbered-list" data-ghq-card-content-type="NUMBERED_LIST" start="1">
  <li class="ghq-card-content__numbered-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="NUMBERED_LIST_ITEM" id="tyjxncyg1y9f">
   ‚ùó Customer receives:
   <em class="ghq-card-content__italic" data-ghq-card-content-type="ITALIC">
    ‚ÄúYour maximum withdrawal amount is exceeded‚Äù
   </em>
  </li>
  <li class="ghq-card-content__numbered-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="NUMBERED_LIST_ITEM" id="Bc79C3NMrtKp">
   ‚ùó Customer receives:
   <em class="ghq-card-content__italic" data-ghq-card-content-type="ITALIC">
    ‚ÄúYou can‚Äôt make a transfer to this currency‚Äù
   </em>
  </li>
 </ol>
 <h2 class="ghq-card-content__medium-heading" data-ghq-card-content-type="MEDIUM_HEADING" id="e0BptxV7LSQd">
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   üìû
  </strong>
  Wio Care Steps
 </h2>
 <h3 class="ghq-card-content__small-heading" data-ghq-card-content-type="SMALL_HEADING" id="7nWT3Z5rlDbv">
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   ‚ö†Ô∏è
  </strong>
  Issue 1: Maximum Withdrawal Limit Exceeded
 </h3>
 <p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="TUxTHaDjGQJT">
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   Customer sees:
  </strong>
 </p>
 <p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="P9drQJ6HZnBk">
  "Your maximum withdrawal amount is exceeded. Please reach out to our customer care for more details."
 </p>
 <p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="OLxHibpkJbL8">
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   Steps to troubleshoot:
  </strong>
 </p>
 <ol class="ghq-card-content__numbered-list" data-ghq-card-content-type="NUMBERED_LIST" start="1">
  <li class="ghq-card-content__numbered-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="NUMBERED_LIST_ITEM" id="5DrDpd67pvOd">
   Open Mambu and check:
  </li>
  <ul class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST">
   <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="RipPp8LLFuL7">
    Customer‚Äôs
    <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
     account status
    </strong>
   </li>
   <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="ZvVlAbcLX5qh">
    <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
     Maximum withdrawal limit
    </strong>
    field
   </li>
  </ul>
  <li class="ghq-card-content__numbered-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="NUMBERED_LIST_ITEM" id="GNYThbMPvbfn">
   If the limit is set to
   <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
    AED 0.01
   </strong>
   , it usually signals a
   <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
    restriction
   </strong>
   due to compliance.
  </li>
 </ol>
 <p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="zTGr8R2gXjL3">
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   Internal for FO Team: Customer account status is Active, but the maximum withdrawal limit is AED 0.01. Kindly connect with the Compliance Ops team to confirm the reason.
  </strong>
 </p>
 <blockquote class="ghq-card-content__block-quote" data-ghq-card-content-type="BLOCK_QUOTE" id="ICk6mYQDmvGU">
  <span class="ghq-card-content__text-color" data-ghq-card-content-type="TEXT_COLOR" style="color:#2f3ba2">
   <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
    Smart Response:
   </strong>
  </span>
  <span class="ghq-card-content__text-color" data-ghq-card-content-type="TEXT_COLOR" style="color:#2f3ba2">
   "Hi! üëã We noticed your withdrawal limit is currently set very low. We're checking this with our team and will update you shortly. Thanks for your patience! üôè"
  </span>
 </blockquote>
 <h3 class="ghq-card-content__small-heading" data-ghq-card-content-type="SMALL_HEADING" id="U30hC7ilhGTQ">
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   ‚ö†Ô∏è
  </strong>
  Issue 2: Currency Transfer Blocked
 </h3>
 <p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="mbFJPETxBvRk">
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   Customer sees:
  </strong>
 </p>
 <p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="1V2nXGb5H81r">
  "You can‚Äôt make a transfer to this currency. Please reach out to our customer care for more details."
 </p>
 <p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="ZUjBFuHuDtrc">
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   Steps to troubleshoot:
  </strong>
 </p>
 <ol class="ghq-card-content__numbered-list" data-ghq-card-content-type="NUMBERED_LIST" start="1">
  <li class="ghq-card-content__numbered-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="NUMBERED_LIST_ITEM" id="9uNPPtwqH3xt">
   Check the customer‚Äôs
   <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
    account status
   </strong>
   in Mambu.
  </li>
  <li class="ghq-card-content__numbered-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="NUMBERED_LIST_ITEM" id="pjlZJ2F29f3T">
   Verify if the currency is listed under
   <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
    restricted/excluded currencies
   </strong>
   (typically for compliance).
  </li>
 </ol>
 <p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="IL1MdqQt7f9z">
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   Internal for FO Team: Based on Mambu, the customer's profile includes restricted currencies. Please verify with the Compliance Ops team for further details.
  </strong>
 </p>
 <blockquote class="ghq-card-content__block-quote" data-ghq-card-content-type="BLOCK_QUOTE" id="7knI64Yess8o">
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   <span class="ghq-card-content__text-color" data-ghq-card-content-type="TEXT_COLOR" style="color:#2f3ba2">
    Smart Response:
   </span>
  </strong>
  <span class="ghq-card-content__text-color" data-ghq-card-content-type="TEXT_COLOR" style="color:#2f3ba2">
   "Hi! üëã It looks like this currency isn‚Äôt available for transfers on your account at the moment. We‚Äôre checking the details and will get back to you soon. Thanks for bearing with us! üôè"
  </span>
 </blockquote>
 <p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="OtL0QKJHEc2U">
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   Service Request:
  </strong>
 </p>
 <div class="ghq-card-content__table-responsive-wrapper">
  <div class="ghq-card-content__table-scroller">
   <table class="ghq-card-content__table" data-ghq-card-content-is-full-width="true" data-ghq-card-content-type="TABLE" data-ghq-table-column-widths="187,160,160" data-ghq-table-header="true">

       <p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="E5hMo2vFVwpJ">
        Topic
       </p>
      </td>
      <td class="ghq-card-content__table-cell" data-ghq-card-content-type="TABLE_CELL">
       <p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="gO30pf31CMS5">

       </p>
      </td>
      <td class="ghq-card-content__table-cell" data-ghq-card-content-type="TABLE_CELL">

<h1 class="ghq-card-content__large-heading" data-ghq-card-content-type="LARGE_HEADING" id="UjJiHKmQCmMG">
 Frequently asked Questions (FAQ's)
</h1>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph ghq-is-empty" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="JJfvZHHGIB92">
</p>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="RXP7yD9RkDHT">
 <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
  1. Can I receive an inward transfer in SGD, EGP, and AUD currencies into on of my multi currency accounts?
 </strong>
</p>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="h5nw71D0l7aZ">
 Unfortunately, the payment will fail if you attempt to transfer funds in a local currency, such as SGD (Singapore Dollar), directly to a USD account into your Wio Personal or Wio Business.
</p>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="ljB7dLhnqn7z">
 The available currencies for receiving funds in a USD account are strictly limited to USD, EUR, and GBP.
</p>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="dzXjfRhlX1no">
 However, if the funds are exchanged by a correspondent bank to USD before reaching the customer's USD account, the payment may successfully arrive in the USD account.
</p>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="XuPv1qG7P2xL">
 <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
  The payment flow will be as follows:
 </strong>
</p>
<ul class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST">
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="PmrdfsVDPwpX">
  A transfer is initiated from the sender's bank in SGD.
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="zAdbuAadetDT">
  Correspondent banks (either the sender's bank or WIO's correspondent) will manage the exchange to USD, which may incur foreign exchange losses.
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="HzYdbXXfX6rC">
  The customer will receive the funds as expected in their USD account.
 </li>
</ul>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph ghq-is-empty" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="FFLrnD4M2om2">
</p>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="oVmZnFLDfbvX">
 <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
  2. What are the key differences between SWIFT and Wise transactions when using Wio?
 </strong>
</p>
<ul class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST">
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="31TMfnIOIIR3">
  SWIFT transactions process major currencies such as Euro (EUR), British Pound (GBP), and US Dollar (USD) using the SWIFT banking network, which offers standardized and secure international transfers.
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="1tV7B5Z7hUE3">
  Wise transactions are utilized for local currencies like the Canadian Dollar (CAD) and Argentine Peso (ARS), with Wise payments only available through AED accounts. USD accounts exclusively handle SWIFT transfers.
 </li>
</ul>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph ghq-is-empty" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="I7JHT5HBSHAj">
</p>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="z77777xRhxoG">
 <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
  3. What is SEPA and the European Economic Area (EEA)
 </strong>
</p>
<ul class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST">
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="Jxt7fa90oc6P">
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   <span class="ghq-card-content__text-color" data-ghq-card-content-type="TEXT_COLOR" style="color:#9013fe">
    What is EEA?
   </span>
  </strong>
  The term
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   EEA
  </strong>
  in the context of SWIFT payments refers to the
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   European Economic Area
  </strong>
  . The EEA includes countries that are part of the European Union (EU) as well as some non-EU countries that have agreed to participate in the EU's single market. In SWIFT payments, transactions involving EEA countries may have specific regulations or conditions due to their participation in the EU's financial systems and markets.
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="dHhhUFRgXa5R">
  <span class="ghq-card-content__text-color" data-ghq-card-content-type="TEXT_COLOR" style="color:#9013fe">
   <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
    What is SEPA?
   </strong>
  </span>
  SEPA is a Europe-wide payment network that allows customers and businesses to make fast, secure cross-border bank transactions. The SEPA zone was established to support the European Union‚Äôs (EU) single market.
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="PfPUO77XwGzk">
  <span class="ghq-card-content__text-color" data-ghq-card-content-type="TEXT_COLOR" style="color:#9013fe">
   <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
    List of SEPA countries:
   </strong>
  </span>
  All 27 EU member states (Austria, Belgium, Bulgaria, Croatia, Cyprus, the Czech Republic, Denmark, Estonia, Finland, France, Germany, Greece, Hungary, Ireland, Italy, Latvia, Lithuania, Luxembourg, Malta, the Netherlands, Poland, Portugal, Romania, Slovakia, Slovenia, Spain, and Sweden) are SEPA countries, as well as Switzerland, the UK, San Marino, Vatican City, Andorra, Monaco, and the three EEA countries of Iceland, Norway, and Liechtenstein. The Europe-wide standardized procedures for cashless payment transactions can be used in all of these countries.
 </li>
</ul>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="jPpvDFWsZALL">
 <span class="ghq-card-content__image-container">

 </span>
</p>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph ghq-is-empty" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="9FVrx1xvZANF">
</p>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="rK53GTvtXtv1">
 <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
  4. What is the limit for receiving inward transfers or payments?
 </strong>
</p>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="9FVrx1xvZANF">
 Customers may receive an unlimited amount through local or international transfers.
</p>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph ghq-is-empty" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="HwbXxhZoYq58">
</p>
